Children's playground: The hotel's indoor and outdoor areas include various small projects in the children's playground, which can satisfy children aged 2 to 4 years old to play freely. The safety and hardware facilities are also very satisfactory.

InterContinental members can also get a welcome gift, a 10% discount on restaurant meals, etc.

It is really worthwhile to avoid the peak period of May Day to check in and play. There is no takeaway nearby. Most of our meals are solved by the hotel. Every time we go to eat, we can meet Tracy Zhou in the restaurant. The service attitude is very good.
